3. The child was very hungry in the morning, and our family was the second table in the restaurant. I was afraid that the staff forgot to tell the staff twice, and the staff were very indifferent. As a result, they got the order wrong and didn't serve us until the eighth table. I didn‚Äôt want to give the children food that had already been cooked, such as steamed buns, corn, and sweet potatoes, because they were all cold when they were brought out with the noodles.
4. This B&B accepts group travel agencies, and the travel agency‚Äôs team has priority. Individual travelers who book rooms on Ctrip are not recommended to come.
5. As a hotel with a pure wooden structure, once a fire occurs, it will be a major accident. The fire escape equipment in the room is fixed and poses a safety hazard. When the escape door on the first floor opens, there is a construction site filled with rocks.

There are two advantages. One is the beautiful view from the hotel courtyard observation deck, and the other is the good service attitude of the housekeeper at the reception.

This is the worst hotel I have stayed in during my trip to Guizhou. I recommend lowering the price to 700 before booking a room. I recommend other B&Bs on my trip, Xiaoqikong Fuyunshanshe and Anshun Yueshan. I and my family are very satisfied.

In addition, the hotel offered me a discount on the room rate but I refused. I don‚Äôt know if other good reviews were obtained in this way.
